 \]\]><!\[CDATA\[ Senior Automation & Controls Engineer (34295) \]\]>**Senior Automation & Controls Engineer**

**Location: Kansas City, MO (On-site/field)**

**Benefits:** Access to Clients Benefits Package

**Description:**

The Senior Automation & Controls Engineer leads and executes Automation and Controls Engineering design activities for minor to major scale Engineering, Procurement, and Construction (EPC) projects in food, consumer products, pharmaceutical, life science, aerospace and industrial facilities. Responsible for executing automation and controls deliverables for project(s) in the front end, detailed design, construction, and start-up phases. Projects range from controls projects working directly for the client to control self-execution on full-scale Automation and Controls EPC projects.

**Responsibilities:**

- Design responsibility for all Automation and Controls scope on the project.

- Leads a team of Automation and Controls Engineers, Specialists, and Designers in the execution of design. Interfaces with a multi-faceted project team internally consisting of project manager, electrical, controls, estimating, procurement, construction, and other engineering disciplines.

- Responsible for leading and developing software design deliverables including PLC and HMI programming design deliverables as well as Batch, MES, servers and virtualization.

- Responsible for commissioning and startup of those design deliverables.

- Lead and prepare controls design deliverables, including instrument/device list, I/O list, controls narratives, control panel and controls hardware design, device location plan drawings and installation details.

- Lead the specification, design, and procurement activities for control panel and equipment vendors, manage vendor progression, and lead the Factory Acceptance Tests (FATs).

- Lead and prepare electrical design deliverables including 480VAC and below equipment and motor power design, installation plan drawings, and conductor schedules.

- Determine process instrument measurements protocols, such as temperature, pressure, flow, level, analyzers, and control valves. Utilize knowledge of various technologies for selecting the appropriate controls application.

- Experienced in reviewing P&IDs and working with process engineers to define and show proper controls scope of the project.

- Develop and manage verification of design, calculations, project studies and report preparation.

- Interfaces directly with offsite design office and coordinates and tracks execution of controls deliverables to that office.

- Responsible for leading and performing quality reviews of project design submittals and coordinating those reviews within the department.

- Responsible for applying knowledge of commonly used automation and controls engineering/design concepts, principles, practices, codes, and procedures within the engineering services industry.

- Interfaces directly with construction personnel in development of contracts and execution of work.

- Develops project estimates at each project phase through various software such as Proposal works, Integrated Architecture Builder (IAB), SIL Solver, Bluebeam, Excel, and Visio.

- Supports project manager in the development and tracking of automation and controls project budgets and expected progress.

- Works with clients and vendors directly in developing design. Build effective relationships with existing clients, customers and contractors and develop new business opportunities. Responsible for ensuring customer satisfaction goals and expectations are met. Have a list of clients that frequently request them for projects or assistance.

- Provides leadership, technical direction and development to Automation and Controls team members.

- Assists in the day-to-day allocation of resources to their projects.

- Coordinate with field personnel to resolve design related installation issues, calculations, field inspections and testing of controls systems.

- Responsible for leading the technical execution and team during onsite start-up and commissioning activities.

- Responsible for developing and submitting discipline change notices as needed to the project management team.

- Fully understands and can execute the EPC project approach.

- This position will require making trips to job sites to survey, support installations, and lead startups

- Work with our business development team to identify and develop key projects and customer pursuits.

- Frequently attends and hosts client events.

- Develop business strategies for future projects. Understands business needs and profitability factors.

- Reviews and develop engineering hour estimates and proposals for all phases of the project.

- Supports interviewing and hiring process for new team members.

- Coordinates workload with Automation and Controls Department Manager.


**Requirements:**

- Bachelor’s degree in Controls, Electrical, Mechanical or Chemical Engineering, or related degree and successful completion of Fundamentals of Engineering (FE) exam

- **7+ years electrical engineering experience**. (6 years with a Masters Degree)

- EPC project and Automation 7 Controls experience are preferred.

- Experience with leading the discipline design for large projects and delegating work tasks to team members.

- Ability to lead execution of work and resolve issues in a team environment.

- Demonstrated critical thinking skills, ability to work methodically and analytically in a quantitative problem-solving environment.

- Strong attention to detail, facilitation, team building, collaboration, organization and problem-solving skills.

- Ability to perform quality reviews for detailed engineering documents and specifications.

- Must have or be able to obtain a Transportation Worker Identification Card (TWIC).

- Professional Engineer (PE) License Preferred

**ESSENTIAL DUTIES AND RESPONSIBILITIES:**

- Lead the engineering team on selecting and sizing equipment for fluid handling systems such as pumps, piping, valves, instrumentation, etc.
- Direct team to create 3D SolidWorks layouts (general arrangements), P&IDs, structural drawings, mechanical assembly drawings, and others as needed to support the production floor.
- Coordinate with the manufacturing shop on all fabricated, pre-assembled, and manufactured system designs.
- Technical resource and decision-making authority to guide designs for safety, manufacturability, reliability, and within budgets.
- Act as an independent project manager of key accounts as required.
- Select engineered equipment to be used in engineered product design.
- Review/ create project proposals that accurately depict offerings to our client.
- Proficient at guiding facility layouts due to maintenance, reliability, and serviceability needs.
- Review mechanical and electrical manufacturing for accuracy and intended function based on the project design.
- Liaison between the engineering/ design team and the production team
- Coordinate material take-offs for purchase of all materials required for fabrication and installation of provided prefabricated and unitized systems.
- Ability to review industry documents to guide designs, including ASME, ANSI, NEC, NFPA, ASTM, customer specifications, and further as required.

**EDUCATION & EXPERIENCE**

- Bachelor's degree in mechanical engineering or technical engineering, math, or science is required.
- 5+ plus years of experience with each of the following:
  - Engineering design
  - Engineering management role with direct reports
  - Oil & gas surface equipment
  - Mechanical systems and associated components (i.e. pumps, piping, and instrumentation)
  - Working as an independent project manager
  -  SolidWorks
- EIT registration is preferred.
- Experience developing/ reviewing drawings for manufacturing of industrial equipment is required
- SolidWorks and AutoCAD, 3D, 2D drafting experience beyond a basic level is required.
- Experience with selection and specification of engineered equipment is required
- Mechanical aptitude and hands-on experience is strongly preferred.
- Microsoft Office proficiency
- Proactive communicator that manages customer and vendor relationships.
- Effective time management skills, personal conduct, and change management abilities.
- Ability to lead a team of engineers and provide mentorship for individual technical and organization growth.

<description>

<!\[CDATA\[ We are looking for a Performance &amp; Optimization Specialist for one of our clients to perform network performance, monitoring, and analysis by collecting and analyzing information, identifying the abnormalities from sources in the domain of the customer solution, diagnosing root causes of performance issues, and recommending improvement for optimization actions (i.e., QoS Optimization, parameter tuning, SW Upgrades, etc.) to meet contractual KPI targets. They find problems that were not identified during testing. In addition to diagnosing network performance issues, the Performance &amp; Optimization Specialist generates daily/weekly/monthly reports related to technology aspects of the customer solution. The specialist performs short-term capacity utilization and traffic pattern assessments to evaluate impact on current and future architecture and recommend optimal network strategy for future traffic/capacity needs, leveraging automation techniques to reduce analysis time and other optimization related activities that involve repetition.<br>\
Required Soft skills:<br>\
a) Strong communication skills<br>\
b) Self starter who will use own deep technical expertise to assess the network configuration and come up with feature/parameter trial plan independently.<br>\
c) Ability to interact/engage customer for technical discussions, review of technical reports/analysis/recommendations<br>\
d) NAM Time zone support<br>\
<br>\
Required Technical Skill Set:<br>\
1\. Strong understanding of 5G NSA, SA (FDD &amp; TDD) and LTE.<br>\
2\. Past hands-on experience with trials/optimization projects for 5G NSA/SA with demonstrated experience on 5G Features for Coverage optimization (e.g. SRS Beamforming), Throughput optimization, Load balancing, layering and Traffic Steering from low to high bands..<br>\
3\. Past hands-on experience with trials/optimization projects for LTE with demonstrated experience on 4G Features for Data/VoLTE Drop call improvement, Load balancing, Layering and Traffic Steering from low to high bands.<br>\
4\. Ability to analyze internal syslogs, eNB/gNB EMIL/DCAP logs, TTI traces for quick troubleshooting and issue resolution for lab or field activities.<br>\
5\. Expertise with UE and eNB/gNB signaling log analysis (UU, X2, S1 signaling)<br>\
6\. Exposure with UE logging tools such as QXDM, XCAL, or equivalent and should be proficient with those tools.<br>\
7\. Experience with Actix post processing of DT logs.<br>\
<br>\
Job Responsibilities<br>\
1\. Performs critical (sometimes escalated) design and performance activities in customer projects independently (complex problem solving in projects and multi-vendor environments).<br>\
2\. Develops / Reviews and makes recommendations on network-wide Design covering Performance, Spectrum &amp; Capacity supported by Recommendations (within and across the region).<br>\
3\. Organizes field measurements and laboratory tests. Performs network audits, especially in cases where fault or problems exist.<br>\
4\. Optimizes networks with all components based on traffic trends and customer forecasts.<br>\
5\. Supports experts in developing network configuration file and interface analysis<br>\
<br>\
Project Specific Roles<br>\
1\. I. LTE LMS assessment and LTE Features evaluation and executing trials for Load balancing, traffic steering campaigns for movement from low to high bands.<br>\
II. LTE and VoLTE Drop call rate improvement via troubleshooting configuration issues, analysis of counters and coming up with trial plan for KPI improvement based on feature trials and parameter tuning (not look for RF shaping skillset)<br>\
III. 5G LMS assessment and 5G Features evaluation and executing trials for 5G DL/UL Throughput improvement, Coverage improvement and traffic steering from low to high bands.<br>\
IV. Troubleshooting hot topics via OSS KPIs, TTI traces, EMIL traces etc<br> \]\]>

<description>

<!\[CDATA\[ <span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;">Myticas is seeking a highly skilled and motivated ASIC Product Engineer to join our clients team. The successful candidate will be responsible for developing specifications and validation methods for Analog ASICs used in datacenter transceiver products. This role involves close collaboration with multiple teams on product definition, requirements, specifications, DVT, qualification, test, and production ramp-up. The ideal candidate will be proactive, able to anticipate problems, and devise effective solutions.</span></span><br>\
<span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;"> </span></span><br>\
<br>\
<span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;"> </span></span><br>\
<span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;"><strong>HOW YOU WILL CONTRIBUTE AND WHAT YOU WILL LEARN</strong></span></span>\
<ul>\
<li style="margin: 0.0cm 0.0cm 8.0pt;"><span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;">Translate system requirements for datacenter communication ICs into detailed specifications and ensure compliance through design, test, and validation processes.</span></span>\
<li style="margin: 0.0cm 0.0cm 8.0pt;"><span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;">Develop and maintain application notes to support the integration of these ICs.</span></span>\
<li style="margin: 0.0cm 0.0cm 8.0pt;"><span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;">Serve as the liaison between the ASIC design team and module-level HW integration and test teams.</span></span>\

<p>We’re looking for a seasoned <strong>FPGA / Hardware Design Engineer</strong> to help architect and deliver next-generation solutions for high-performance video and data applications. <description>

<!\[CDATA\[ <p>You will be responsible for the development of integrated circuits operating at speeds greater than 100Gbaud for next-generation products. This role involves driving multiple aspects of IC product development, including circuit design, physical layout, and silicon bring-up. You will collaborate closely with teams across verification, CAD, product engineering, and test engineering to create and execute detailed design validation test (DVT) plans and device characterization strategies.</p>\

<description>

<!\[CDATA\[ <span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;"><strong><span style="font-size: 18.0pt;">FPGA / Hardware Design Engineer</span></strong></span></span><br>\
\
<p>We are seeking an FPGA/Hardware Engineer to help design and optimize advanced media transport and processing systems for high-performance video, audio, and data applications. This role involves hands-on design, testing, and support of production-grade solutions.</p>\
\
<h3>Key Responsibilities</h3>\
\
<ul>\
<li>\
<p>Develop FPGA-based solutions for video/audio transport and real-time processing (SMPTE ST 2110/IP, SDI).</p>\
<li>\
<p>Implement and optimize RTL designs, with a focus on 4K performance, data compression, and parallel processing.</p>\
<li>\
<p>Support hardware testing, debugging, and validation in lab environments.</p>\
<li>\
<p>Contribute to new product introduction (NPI) through design, documentation, and test activities.</p>\
<li>\
<p>Collaborate with cross-functional teams on requirements, component selection, and technical documentation.</p>\
</ul>\
\
<h3>What We’re Looking For</h3>\
\
<ul>\
<li>\
<p>2+ years of FPGA or hardware design experience (video/audio focus preferred).</p>\
<li>\
<p>Hands-on experience with Intel and/or Xilinx FPGA platforms and design tools.</p>\
<li>\
<p>Proficiency with SystemVerilog (preferred), VHDL, or HLS; scripting in TCL/SDC.</p>\
<li>\
<p>Familiarity with high-speed interfaces (Ethernet, DDR), transceivers, and timing analysis.</p>\
<li>\
<p>Strong problem-solving, debugging, and communication skills.</p>\
</ul>\

<description>

<!\[CDATA\[ <p>We are seeking an experienced and highly skilled Senior Network Architect with expertise in Segment Routing to join our dynamic and innovative team. As a Senior Network Architect, you will play a pivotal role in designing, implementing, and optimizing our network infrastructure, with a specific focus on segment routing technologies. Your deep understanding of network architecture, protocols, and best practices will contribute to the scalability, reliability, and performance of our network while ensuring alignment with business objectives.</p>\
\
<p><br>\
The Sr. Network Architect is a Subject Matter Expert (SME) on all aspects of the LEO Network design and works with other LEO teams within Telesat and external contractors to ensure designs, implementation decisions, validation plans and documentation reflect the business requirements and objectives of the LEO program.</p>\
\
<h2>Main Responsibilities</h2>\
\
<ul>\
<li>Segment Routing Design and Implementation:</li>\
<li>Participate in the design and implementation of segment routing solutions, ensuring optimal utilization of network resources and improved traffic engineering.</li>\
<li>Collaborate with cross-functional teams to understand business requirements and translate them into effective network solution designs.</li>\
<li>Develop strategies for partner business units to implement and manage network services implementations of segment routing architectures.</li>\
<li>Network Architecture and Optimization:</li>\
<li>Contribute to the architectural planning and evolution of the network, incorporating segment routing as a key technology.</li>\
<li>Identify opportunities for optimization and enhanced performance using segment routing techniques, such as traffic steering, BSIDs and fast reroute mechanisms.</li>\
<li>Perform network assessments and recommend improvements to maintain network health and operational efficiency.</li>\
<li>Represent the LEO Network Engineering team by documenting and delivering network requirements to hardware and software development teams specifically in the areas of customer facing MEF 3.0 interface and networking design support requirements on data processing equipment</li>\
<li>In coordination with Network team attend, contribute and produce materials for internal and external design and system engineering reviews for LEO Network Engineering related activities</li>\
<li>Protocols and Standards:</li>\
<li>Maintain a deep understanding of industry standards and protocols related to segment routing, such as IS-IS, BGP, and MPLS.</li>\
<li>Stay updated with emerging trends and advancements in segment routing technologies, applying them to enhance network capabilities.</li>\
<li>Troubleshooting and Problem Resolution:</li>\
<li>Act as a subject matter expert, assist with complex network troubleshooting and incident resolution.</li>\
<li>Collaborate with the LEO team to diagnose and address network behaviors and incidents in a timely manner, minimizing service disruptions.</li>\
<li>Vendor and Solution Evaluation:</li>\
<li>Evaluate new networking hardware, software, and solutions that align with segment routing strategies and network growth plans.</li>\
<li>Collaborate with vendors to understand product roadmaps and provide feedback for feature enhancements.</li>\
<li>Documentation and Knowledge Sharing:</li>\
<li>Create and maintain detailed technical documentation, including network diagrams, configuration guidelines, and troubleshooting procedures related to segment routing.</li>\
<li>Prepare and deliver materials including presentations, reference documentation and test strategies for LEO network equipment and applications deployment and operation</li>\
<li>Share knowledge and mentor junior team members, fostering a culture of continuous learning and skill development.</li>\
<li>With LEO Network Engineers develop and oversee plans including product idea investigations, proof of concept, Service validation and product demonstrations in Telesat LEO labs</li>\
</ul>\
\
<h2>Education and Experience</h2>\
\
<ul>\
<li>10+ years of experience in carrier network design, operation and deployment</li>\
<li>Broad experience or exposure across all areas of network related product design, development, verification, deployment and support</li>\
<li>Understanding of Metro Ethernet Forum (MEF) standards and objectives as they relate to Carrier Ethernet Services.</li>\
<li>Knowledge of routing and switching protocols, including BGP, OSPF, IS-IS, and MPLS.</li>\
<li>Experience with network automation and scripting using tools such as Python, Ansible, or similar.</li>\
<li>Strong troubleshooting skills and the ability to diagnose and resolve complex network issues.</li>\
<li>Demonstrated leadership skills and the ability to guide and mentor junior engineers.</li>\
<li>In-depth understanding of security principles and practices as they relate to network architecture.</li>\
<li>Proven experience in network design, architecture, and optimization.</li>\
<li>Professional certifications such as Cisco CCIE, Juniper JNCIE, or equivalent, are highly desirable.</li>\
<li>Comfortable leading meetings and able to communicate issues and trends to senior management and other groups at the appropriate level of detail.</li>\
<li>Excellent communication (verbal, written, presentation) and interpersonal skills.</li>\
<li>Excellent communication and collaboration abilities, with a proven track record of working effectively within cross-functional teams.</li>\
<li>Communicates well with own team and across organizational boundaries to ensure the successful completion of shared goals.</li>\
</ul> \]\]>

<description>

<!\[CDATA\[ <p>One of Myticas Consulting's direct clients is seeking a Cybersecurity Analyst for a 100% Remote contract position.<br>\
<br>\
<strong>Duration:</strong> 12+ months contract (possible further extension).<br>\
<strong>NOTE:</strong> Must be a US Citizen.<br>\
<br>\
<strong>Job Summary:</strong><br>\
One of our direct clients Cyber Security Program Office (CSPO) is looking for a Sr Cybersecurity<strong> </strong>Analyst who will play an important role to continuously monitor, triage alerts and tickets, investigate suspicious activity or poor configurations, and orchestrate responses to protect the client’s systems and data.<br>\
<br>\
<strong><u>Typical tasks may include:</u></strong></p>\
\
<ul>\
<li>Resetting user passwords for cause (e.g., when they have been identified as being suspected compromised or ‘known compromised’).\
<li>Working with service owners to reset service account passwords for various reasons.\
<li>Ensuring authorizers are designated for in-scope accounts.\
<li>Analyzing usage patterns for accounts (e.g., service, administrative) to identify inactive accounts or inappropriate account use.\
<li>Reviewing approval requests for various new access or accounts.\
<li>Triaging unusual access requests (e.g., access from 3rd party VPN providers, impossible travel) or phishing reports.\
<li>Evaluate endpoint and detection response (EDR) installation and coverage.\
<li>Identify systems without EDR and provide to IT teams for remediation.\
<li>Monitoring external attack surface for unapproved systems, undocumented systems, and newly disclosed vulnerabilities.\
<li>Reviewing systems with existing public access to ensure requirements for these systems are followed (e.g., event logging, multifactor authentication).\
<li>Attend online/Teams meetings with team and others as appropriate.\
<li>Work with team to provide status on current task, suggest improvements, discuss implementation, etc.\
</ul>\
\
<p><br>\
<strong><em>Minimum Qualifications:</em></strong></p>\
\
<ul>\
<li>1–3 years in a SOC, cybersecurity ‘blue team’, or closely related role.\
<li>3–5 years relevant experience including investigations, data analysis, and detection tuning.\
<li>Comfort using Splunk Processing Language (SPL), CrowdStrike EDR, and ServiceNow.\
<li>Strong grasp of TCP/IP, OSI model, and common protocols (HTTP, DNS, SMTP). Windows/Linux/macOS fundamentals; Active Directory/Azure AD concepts; basic cloud logging.\
<li>Experience with at least one SIEM and one EDR/XDR platform.\
<li>Experience with ticketing/case management.\
<li>Ability to craft queries using common languages; comfort with regex, JSON and APIs; basic scripting in Python/PowerShell/Bash.\
<li>Excellent analytical, problem-solving, and communication skills both with stakeholders, peers, and internal customers; able to operate under pressure in a shift or on-call environment.\
</ul>\
\
<ul>\
</ul> \]\]>

<description>

<!\[CDATA\[ <p><strong>Myticas's direct client, based in Riverwoods, IL or Philadelphia, PA, is currently seeking a Accounting Manager</strong> <strong>for a hybrid contract to hire position.</strong></p>\
\
<p> </p>\
\
<p><strong>Additional Information</strong><strong>:</strong>  W2 only!</p>\
\
<ul>\
<li>Hybrid position - 2 to 3 days per week onsite, open to candidates local to Philadelphia, PA or Riverwoods, IL\
<li>This is a Temp-to-Hire Position\
</ul>\
\
<p><strong>Job Description:</strong></p>\
\
<p>The Accounting Manager plays a critical role in overseeing the accounting and financial reporting functions, ensuring accuracy, timeliness, and compliance with internal controls. This position requires a detail-oriented, analytical thinker with strong leadership capabilities and the ability to navigate complex accounting scenarios proactively.<br>\
<br>\
<strong>ESSENTIAL DUTIES AND RESPONSIBILITIES:</strong><br>\
• Lead and support the month-end close and reporting process in alignment with the reporting calendar.<br>\
• Supervise and mentor accounting staff, providing guidance, performance feedback, and support to improve processes — including the quality of account reconciliations.<br>\
• Review, analyze, and approve general ledger transactions to ensure completeness and accuracy.<br>\
• Oversee the preparation and review of balance sheet account reconciliations on a monthly, quarterly, and semi-annual basis.<br>\
• Proactively identify and resolve accounting issues, escalating, when necessary, with recommended solutions.<br>\
• Support internal and external audits by providing requested documentation and addressing inquiries professionally.<br>\
• Maintain and update desktop procedures and checklists to reflect changes in processes and tools.<br>\
• Maintain and monitor month-end close, reporting, and operational checklists to ensure timely and complete task execution before sign-off.<br>\
• Prepare and review supporting schedules and financial analyses as needed.<br>\
• Collaborate effectively with internal teams and third-party service providers to ensure smooth operations.<br>\
• Conduct independent analysis to identify opportunities for process improvement and implement recommendations.<br>\
• Support the timely research and resolution of reconciling items to ensure accuracy and compliance with deadlines.<br>\
• Demonstrate adaptability to changing business requirements and provide leadership and support to staff during transitions.<br>\
• Take initiative in identifying issues and opportunities, follow through on projects, and proactively recommend solutions to improve processes and resolve challenges.<br>\
<br>\
<strong>Required Qualifications/Experience/Skills: </strong><br>\
• 7–9 years of<strong> accounting/audit experience, including 2–3 years in a managerial</strong> role.<br>\
• Ideal candidates must have <strong>current or recent (within the past 1–2 years) experience managing teams responsible for core general ledger functions</strong>. This includes hands-on oversight of month-end close, journal entry preparation and review, balance sheet and bank reconciliations, intercompany transactions, and audit support.<br>\
• <strong>Bachelor’s degree in Accounting (BBA or BS)</strong>; Master’s degree preferred.<br>\
• <strong>CPA certification </strong>or progress toward certification strongly preferred.<br>\
<br>\
<strong>A strong and recent focus on GL is required to be considered for this role:</strong><br>\
• Experience with international accounting is a plus.<br>\
• Proficiency in major <strong>ERP systems (SAP, Great Plains, NetSuite) and Blackline.</strong><br>\
• Advanced skills in <strong>Microsoft Office Suite (Excel, Word, PowerPoint, Access).</strong><br>\
• Strong analytical and problem-solving skills with a detail-oriented approach.<br>\
• Proven ability to manage teams and work independently in a fast-paced environment.<br>\
• Comfortable working wit<strong>h accelerated month-end close timelines (3–5 days).</strong><br>\
• Excellent communication and interpersonal skills to foster cross-functional collaboration.<br>\
• Project management experience is highly desirable.<br>\
• Flexibility to work hybrid hours and coordinate effectively during close/reporting cycles.</p> \]\]>

...

</description>

<description>

<!\[CDATA\[ <p><strong>Myticas's direct client, based in Philadelphia, PA, is currently seeking a Accounting Manager</strong> <strong>for a hybrid contract to hire position.</strong></p>\
\
<p> </p>\
\
<p><strong>Additional Information</strong><strong>:</strong>  W2 only!</p>\
\
<ul>\
<li>Hybrid position - 2 to 3 days per week onsite, open to candidates local to Philadelphia, PA\
<li>This is a Temp-to-Hire Position\
</ul>\
\
<p><strong>Job Description:</strong></p>\
\
<p>The Accounting Manager plays a critical role in overseeing the accounting and financial reporting functions, ensuring accuracy, timeliness, and compliance with internal controls. This position requires a detail-oriented, analytical thinker with strong leadership capabilities and the ability to navigate complex accounting scenarios proactively.<br>\
<br>\
<strong>ESSENTIAL DUTIES AND RESPONSIBILITIES:</strong><br>\
• Lead and support the month-end close and reporting process in alignment with the reporting calendar.<br>\
• Supervise and mentor accounting staff, providing guidance, performance feedback, and support to improve processes — including the quality of account reconciliations.<br>\
• Review, analyze, and approve general ledger transactions to ensure completeness and accuracy.<br>\
• Oversee the preparation and review of balance sheet account reconciliations on a monthly, quarterly, and semi-annual basis.<br>\
• Proactively identify and resolve accounting issues, escalating, when necessary, with recommended solutions.<br>\
• Support internal and external audits by providing requested documentation and addressing inquiries professionally.<br>\
• Maintain and update desktop procedures and checklists to reflect changes in processes and tools.<br>\
• Maintain and monitor month-end close, reporting, and operational checklists to ensure timely and complete task execution before sign-off.<br>\
• Prepare and review supporting schedules and financial analyses as needed.<br>\
• Collaborate effectively with internal teams and third-party service providers to ensure smooth operations.<br>\
• Conduct independent analysis to identify opportunities for process improvement and implement recommendations.<br>\
• Support the timely research and resolution of reconciling items to ensure accuracy and compliance with deadlines.<br>\
• Demonstrate adaptability to changing business requirements and provide leadership and support to staff during transitions.<br>\
• Take initiative in identifying issues and opportunities, follow through on projects, and proactively recommend solutions to improve processes and resolve challenges.<br>\
<br>\
<strong>Required Qualifications/Experience/Skills: </strong><br>\
• 7–9 years of<strong> accounting/audit experience, including 2–3 years in a managerial</strong> role.<br>\
• Ideal candidates must have <strong>current or recent (within the past 1–2 years) experience managing teams responsible for core general ledger functions</strong>. This includes hands-on oversight of month-end close, journal entry preparation and review, balance sheet and bank reconciliations, intercompany transactions, and audit support.<br>\
• <strong>Bachelor’s degree in Accounting (BBA or BS)</strong>; Master’s degree preferred.<br>\
• <strong>CPA certification </strong>or progress toward certification strongly preferred.<br>\
<br>\
<strong>A strong and recent focus on GL is required to be considered for this role:</strong><br>\
• Experience with international accounting is a plus.<br>\
• Proficiency in major <strong>ERP systems (SAP, Great Plains, NetSuite) and Blackline.</strong><br>\
• Advanced skills in <strong>Microsoft Office Suite (Excel, Word, PowerPoint, Access).</strong><br>\
• Strong analytical and problem-solving skills with a detail-oriented approach.<br>\
• Proven ability to manage teams and work independently in a fast-paced environment.<br>\
• Comfortable working wit<strong>h accelerated month-end close timelines (3–5 days).</strong><br>\
• Excellent communication and interpersonal skills to foster cross-functional collaboration.<br>\
• Project management experience is highly desirable.<br>\
• Flexibility to work hybrid hours and coordinate effectively during close/reporting cycles.</p> \]\]>

<description>

<!\[CDATA\[ <p><span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;"><strong><span style="font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="">EDW Sr. Data Analyst (Federal Reporting)</span></span></strong></span></span><br>\
<br>\
<span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;"><strong><span style="font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="">Job Title: EDW Sr. Data Analyst (Federal Reporting)</span></span></strong></span></span><br>\
<span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;"><strong><span style="font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="">Contract: </span></span></strong><span style="font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="">W2– Candidates must be authorized to work in the U.S. on a W2 basis. We cannot accept candidates requiring sponsorship or those from C2C vendors.</span></span></span></span><br>\
<span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;"><strong><span style="font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="">Duration: </span></span></strong><span style="font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="">12 months with possible multi-year extension/s</span></span></span></span><br>\
<span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;"><strong><span style="font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="">Pay:</span></span></strong><span style="font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style=""> $47 to $53 per hour USD. </span></span></span></span><br>\
<span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;"><strong><span style="font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="">Location:</span></span></strong><span style="font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style=""> Remote – Local Springfield, IL candidates strongly preferred.</span></span></span></span><br>\
<span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;"><em><span style="font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="">This is a telecommute position with some (&lt;15%) required travel to Springfield, IL for onsite customer meetings.</span></span></em></span></span><br>\
<br>\
<span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;"><strong><span style="font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="">Job Summary: </span></span></strong></span></span><br>\
<span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;"><span style="font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="">We are seeking a highly experienced Data Analyst to join our Enterprise Data Warehouse (EDW) federal reporting team. This role is responsible for analyzing healthcare-related data, developing reports, and ensuring data integrity. The ideal candidate will have a deep understanding of the Medicaid program, data analysis, SQL, CMS federal reporting (CMS 64/21) and data warehousing best practices, with a focus on supporting healthcare-related data systems. </span></span></span></span><br>\
<span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;"><strong><span style="font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="">Key Responsibilities: </span></span></strong></span></span></p>\
\
<ul>\
<li style="margin-bottom: 0.0in;margin: 0.0in 0.0in 0.0in 0.5in;"><span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;"><span style="font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="">Analyze healthcare-related data to support business decision-making and CMS federal reporting including but not limited to CMS 64/21 reports. </span></span></span></span>\
<li style="margin-bottom: 0.0in;margin: 0.0in 0.0in 0.0in 0.5in;"><span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;"><span style="font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="">Develop and maintain reports and dashboards using SQL and other BI tools. </span></span></span></span>\
<li style="margin-bottom: 0.0in;margin: 0.0in 0.0in 0.0in 0.5in;"><span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;"><span style="font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="">Collaborate with stakeholders to gather requirements and recommend technical solutions. </span></span></span></span>\

This role provides the guidance and direction to support a large data warehouse implementation and operations. The selected SME will provide the required decisions for the business and technical team members to modify, change, enhance or correct within the system, related to claims, provider, and recipient data. </span></span></span><br>\

This is a telecommute position with some (&lt;25%) required travel to Springfield, IL for onsite customer meetings. </span></span></span><br>\

<span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;"><span style="font-size: 10.0pt;">Clover Consulting, a Myticas Co., is seeking a <strong>Manufacturing Engineer</strong> to be an Associate to the Senior Manufacturing Engineer.  In this position, you will lead and provide ongoing support through our manufacturing life cycle!</span></span></span><br>\
<br>\
<span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;"><span style="font-size: 10.0pt;">This is a 12 month contract opportunity, with great likelihood for Contract to Hire. This is a<strong> first shift position, hours are 7am to 4pm.</strong></span></span></span><br>\
<br>\

Acts as a technical expert in process technology</span></span></span><br>\
<br>\
<span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;"><em><span style="font-size: 10.0pt;">Improvements:</span></em><span style="font-size: 10.0pt;"> Independently, with innovation and creativity, evaluates manufacturing processes to ensure optimal labor and material costs to increase productivity and profitability. Identifies, reduces, and eliminates worker exposure(s) to ergonomic stress(es) in the work place.</span></span></span><br>\
<br>\
<span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;"><em><span style="font-size: 10.0pt;">Floor Support</span></em><span style="font-size: 10.0pt;">: Provides timely product and process support for any manufacturing area to diagnose problems and implement solutions to minimize interruptions to production.</span></span></span><br>\

<span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;"><strong><u>SUMMARY</u></strong></span></span><br>\
<br>\
<span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;">The Project Manager will lead and motivate a team in the day-to-day management of project safety, quality, schedule, cost control, contracts, risk, suppliers, proposals, estimates, documentation turnover, client relations/management, field staff and other duties required to execute Design-Only, Engineer Procure Construct (EPC), Construction Management, Construction, and Program Management projects. They will lead projects from inception to completion and may perform the role of EPC Project Manager or Program Manager, as well as provide guidance to others performing these roles as required by the specific project. They will be responsible for overall project execution and successful completion of projects on time and within budget.</span></span><br>\
<br>\
<span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;"><strong><u>Responsibilities</u></strong></span></span><br>\
\
<ul>\
<li style="margin: 0.0in 0.0in 0.0in 0.5in;"><span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;">Provide leadership and guidance of all aspects of multi-discipline engineering projects from concept to completion, including overall safety, quality, engineering, procurement, construction, environmental compliance, project controls, and public/community relations.</span></span>\
<li style="margin: 0.0in 0.0in 0.0in 0.5in;"><span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;">Establish project teams, coordinate activities of multiple disciplines, and ensure the efficient, cost-effective utilization of staff.</span></span>\
<li style="margin: 0.0in 0.0in 0.0in 0.5in;"><span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;">Manage all aspects of project communication.</span></span>\
<li style="margin: 0.0in 0.0in 0.0in 0.5in;"><span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;">Lead the Project Management team in administering request for proposal (RFP) package development, bid and selection process, and scope of work documents.</span></span>\
<li style="margin: 0.0in 0.0in 0.0in 0.5in;"><span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;">Develop and monitor project schedules, manage scope, and control project costs.</span></span>\
<li style="margin: 0.0in 0.0in 0.0in 0.5in;"><span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;">Serve as the primary point of contact for clients regarding efforts such as client coordination, strategic planning, master scope management, budget finances, subcontracting, project staffing, environmental compliance, facility support and schedule attainment.</span></span>\
<li style="margin: 0.0in 0.0in 0.0in 0.5in;"><span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;">Manage the review, negotiation, approval, and execution of prime contracts, subcontracts, and change orders.</span></span>\
<li style="margin: 0.0in 0.0in 0.0in 0.5in;"><span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;">Lead internal and external project risk reviews and consult with Risk Department as required.</span></span>\
<li style="margin: 0.0in 0.0in 0.0in 0.5in;"><span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;">Manage and approve internal and external reports, providing detailed, accurate project cost forecasts and accruals to client(s) and Global Practice leadership as required.</span></span>\
<li style="margin: 0.0in 0.0in 0.0in 0.5in;"><span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;">Manage project controls efforts, including project cost reporting, scheduling, project work breakdown structure establishment, project set-up and closeout within the accounting system, and field progress tracking.</span></span>\
<li style="margin: 0.0in 0.0in 0.0in 0.5in;"><span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;">Monitor progress on projects and provide input into areas of concern and direction or redirection to enhance achievement of project schedules, productivity of goals, budgets, quality, and overall profitability of the project.</span></span>\
<li style="margin: 0.0in 0.0in 0.0in 0.5in;"><span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;">Responsible for managing contract closeout activities.</span></span>\
<li style="margin: 0.0in 0.0in 0.0in 0.5in;"><span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;">Responsible for generating new business revenue by developing new client relationships or leveraging existing client relationships.</span></span>\
<li style="margin: 0.0in 0.0in 0.0in 0.5in;"><span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;">Adhere to safety programs, trainings, and policies, as well as promote and manage the safety and health performance of project team members and subcontractors.</span></span>\
<li style="margin: 0.0in 0.0in 0.0in 0.5in;"><span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;">Participate in and attend industry-associated conferences and/or committees.</span></span>\
<li style="margin: 0.0in 0.0in 0.0in 0.5in;"><span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;">Provide leadership, guidance, and instruction to less experienced staff.</span></span>\
<li style="margin: 0.0in 0.0in 8.0pt 0.5in;"><span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;">Responsible for QA/QC process adherence.</span></span>\
</ul>\
<span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;"><strong><u>Qualifications</u></strong></span></span>\
\
<ul>\
<li style="margin: 0.0in 0.0in 0.0in 0.5in;"><span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;">Bachelor's Degree in Engineering, Construction Management or related degree from an accredited program and 7 years applicable experience required.</span></span>\
<li style="margin: 0.0in 0.0in 0.0in 0.5in;"><span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;">Prior experience on construction project sites or executing program management in the industries of aviation, commercial, energy, government, manufacturing, oil &amp; gas, process, transmission &amp; distribution, or water is preferred.</span></span>\
<li style="margin: 0.0in 0.0in 0.0in 0.5in;"><span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;">Excellent written and verbal communication skills.</span></span>\
<li style="margin: 0.0in 0.0in 0.0in 0.5in;"><span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;">Strong analytical and problem-solving skills, and attention to detail.</span></span>\
<li style="margin: 0.0in 0.0in 0.0in 0.5in;"><span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;">Ability to thrive in a fast-paced, demanding work environment, ability to work overtime on short notice.</span></span>\
<li style="margin: 0.0in 0.0in 0.0in 0.5in;"><span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;">Excellent computer skills and proficiency using Microsoft Office</span></span>\
<li style="margin: 0.0in 0.0in 0.0in 0.5in;"><span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;">Ability to work collaboratively with others (owners, contractors, engineers, designers) in a multi-disciplined project team environment to resolve design or drawing issues as appropriate and to accomplish objectives.</span></span>\
<li style="margin: 0.0in 0.0in 8.0pt 0.5in;"><span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;">Strong experience with document control, scheduling, cost control and project management software</span></span>\
</ul> \]\]>

<description>

<!\[CDATA\[ <strong>Staff Civil Engineer</strong><br>\
Location: Chicago, IL<br>\
Pay Range: $44.00 - $60.50<br>\
Benefits: Standard Medical, Dental, 401(k)<br>\
<br>\
<u><strong>SUMMARY</strong></u><br>\
<br>\
We are looking for experienced a Staff Civil Engineer to support our growing presence in the Great Lakes water market. This is a position with the opportunity to travel across the Chicago region to projects during the construction phase. This position provides the opportunity to grow professionally within one of the industry’s leading firms. Potential projects include drinking water (treatment, storage, and distribution), wastewater (treatment, collection, and conveyance), stormwater (collection, conveyance, detention, and green infrastructure). <br>\
<br>\
The Staff Civil Engineer will perform field activities such as site investigations, inspections, and assessments for projects in a variety of locations. This position provides guidance and direction by utilizing knowledge of standards, specifications, construction plans, document control, applicable codes and Client policies and procedures. Provide Resident Engineering and Inspection of construction projects to ensure contractors are building projects in accordance with project plans, specifications, and industry standards.<br>\
<br>\
<u><strong>Responsibilities</strong></u>\
<ul>\
<li>Create field reports and documentation of daily work performed on project sites.\
<li>Produce accurate quantity data for use in generation of contractor pay estimates and material certification.\
<li>Coordinate with designers as required for shop drawing reviews, requests for information and change orders.\
<li>Maintain communication with Project Managers throughout the course of the project so they are informed of site progress.\
<li>Maintain communication with Section Manager throughout the course of the project regarding project progress and issues.\
<li>Solve technical problems related to the project parameters.\
<li>Interface with clients as needed.\
<li>Ensure compliance with company and site safety policies.\
<li>Have the ability to work productively in an office setting during down time on project sites.\
</ul>\
<u><strong>Requirements</strong></u>\
\
<ul>\
<li>Any of the following education combinations:\
<ul>\
<li>Bachelor's degree in Civil Engineering or related degree from an ABET accredited program AND 3 years of Civil Engineering experience, (consulting preferred).\
<li>Bachelor's degree in Civil or related engineering technology from an ABET accredited program and successful completion of Fundamentals of Engineering (FE) exam AND 3 years of civil engineering experience, consulting preferred required\
<li>Master's degree in Civil Engineering and 2 years of Civil Engineering experience, (consulting preferred).\
</ul>\
<li>Strong knowledge in standard civil engineering techniques and procedures.\
<li>Excellent written and verbal communication skills.\
<li>Ability to work methodically and analytically in a quantitative problem-solving environment and demonstrated critical thinking skills.\
<li>Strong computer skills (e.g. Microsoft Office Suite)\
<li>Strong computer skills (e.g. AutoCAD, MicroStation, BIM (Revit), Civil 3D, PLS, PLS-CADD, RISA-3D, MathCADD), and/or hydraulic, hydrologic, pavement, civil analysis programs.\
<li>Strong attention to detail, facilitation, team building, collaboration, organization and problem-solving skills.\
<li>Engineers in Training-EIT Certification Preferred\
</ul>\
<br>\

<description>

<!\[CDATA\[ <p>Structural Engineer <br>\
Location: Merrillville, Il <br>\
Direct hire<br>\
Can turn into a hybrid role after ramp up period (3 days on site and 2 days remote)<br>\
Salary: 85,000-110,000<br>\
<br>\
We are seeking a <strong>Structural Engineer</strong> to join our growing engineering team. In this role, you will collect and prepare data, perform detailed engineering calculations, and contribute to the design of industrial and infrastructure projects. You’ll collaborate with senior engineers and cross-functional teams to develop creative, cost-effective, and high-quality structural solutions that meet project objectives.</p>\
\
<p>This position offers the opportunity to grow professionally, participate in technical development, and work on meaningful projects that require strong analytical thinking and problem-solving skills.</p>\
\
<hr>\
<h3><strong>Key Responsibilities</strong></h3>\
\
<ul>\
<li>\
<p>Collect and prepare data and perform detailed engineering calculations for assigned projects.</p>\
<li>\
<p>Support fieldwork, inspections, installations, and problem-solving activities.</p>\
<li>\
<p>Collaborate with other departments and external suppliers to obtain technical information.</p>\
<li>\
<p>Manage project scope, address changes, and ensure deliverables are completed on schedule and within budget.</p>\
<li>\

<description>

<!\[CDATA\[ <p><strong>Senior Automation &amp; Controls Engineer</strong><br>\
<strong>Location: Kansas City, MO (On-site/field) </strong></p>\
\
<p><strong>Benefits: </strong>Access to Clients Benefits Package</p>\
\
<p><strong><u>Description: </u></strong></p>\
\
<p>The Senior Automation &amp; Controls Engineer leads and executes Automation and Controls Engineering design activities for minor to major scale Engineering, Procurement, and Construction (EPC) projects in food, consumer products, pharmaceutical, life science, aerospace and industrial facilities. Responsible for executing automation and controls deliverables for project(s) in the front end, detailed design, construction, and start-up phases. Projects range from controls projects working directly for the client to control self-execution on full-scale Automation and Controls EPC projects.</p>\
\
<p><strong><u>Responsibilities:</u></strong></p>\
\
<ul>\
<li>Design responsibility for all Automation and Controls scope on the project.\
<li>Leads a team of Automation and Controls Engineers, Specialists, and Designers in the execution of design. Interfaces with a multi-faceted project team internally consisting of project manager, electrical, controls, estimating, procurement, construction, and other engineering disciplines.\
<li>Responsible for leading and developing software design deliverables including PLC and HMI programming design deliverables as well as Batch, MES, servers and virtualization.\
<li>Responsible for commissioning and startup of those design deliverables.\
<li>Lead and prepare controls design deliverables, including instrument/device list, I/O list, controls narratives, control panel and controls hardware design, device location plan drawings and installation details.\
<li>Lead the specification, design, and procurement activities for control panel and equipment vendors, manage vendor progression, and lead the Factory Acceptance Tests (FATs).\
<li>Lead and prepare electrical design deliverables including 480VAC and below equipment and motor power design, installation plan drawings, and conductor schedules.\
<li>Determine process instrument measurements protocols, such as temperature, pressure, flow, level, analyzers, and control valves. Utilize knowledge of various technologies for selecting the appropriate controls application.\
<li>Experienced in reviewing P&amp;IDs and working with process engineers to define and show proper controls scope of the project.\
<li>Develop and manage verification of design, calculations, project studies and report preparation.\
<li>Interfaces directly with offsite design office and coordinates and tracks execution of controls deliverables to that office.\
<li>Responsible for leading and performing quality reviews of project design submittals and coordinating those reviews within the department.\
<li>Responsible for applying knowledge of commonly used automation and controls engineering/design concepts, principles, practices, codes, and procedures within the engineering services industry.\
<li>Interfaces directly with construction personnel in development of contracts and execution of work.\
<li>Develops project estimates at each project phase through various software such as Proposal works, Integrated Architecture Builder (IAB), SIL Solver, Bluebeam, Excel, and Visio.\
<li>Supports project manager in the development and tracking of automation and controls project budgets and expected progress.\
<li>Works with clients and vendors directly in developing design. Build effective relationships with existing clients, customers and contractors and develop new business opportunities. Responsible for ensuring customer satisfaction goals and expectations are met. Have a list of clients that frequently request them for projects or assistance.\
<li>Provides leadership, technical direction and development to Automation and Controls team members.\
<li>Assists in the day-to-day allocation of resources to their projects.\
<li>Coordinate with field personnel to resolve design related installation issues, calculations, field inspections and testing of controls systems.\
<li>Responsible for leading the technical execution and team during onsite start-up and commissioning activities.\
<li>Responsible for developing and submitting discipline change notices as needed to the project management team.\
<li>Fully understands and can execute the EPC project approach.\
<li>This position will require making trips to job sites to survey, support installations, and lead startups\
<li>Work with our business development team to identify and develop key projects and customer pursuits.\
<li>Frequently attends and hosts client events.\
<li>Develop business strategies for future projects. Understands business needs and profitability factors.\
<li>Reviews and develop engineering hour estimates and proposals for all phases of the project.\
<li>Supports interviewing and hiring process for new team members.\
<li>Coordinates workload with Automation and Controls Department Manager.\
</ul>\
<br>\
<strong><u>Requirements: </u></strong>\
\
<ul>\
<li>Bachelor’s degree in Controls, Electrical, Mechanical or Chemical Engineering, or related degree and successful completion of Fundamentals of Engineering (FE) exam\
<li><strong>7+ years electrical engineering experience</strong>. (6 years with a Masters Degree)\
<li>EPC project and Automation 7 Controls experience are preferred.\
<li>Experience with leading the discipline design for large projects and delegating work tasks to team members.\
<li>Ability to lead execution of work and resolve issues in a team environment.\
<li>Demonstrated critical thinking skills, ability to work methodically and analytically in a quantitative problem-solving environment.\
<li>Strong attention to detail, facilitation, team building, collaboration, organization and problem-solving skills.\
<li>Ability to perform quality reviews for detailed engineering documents and specifications.\
<li>Must have or be able to obtain a Transportation Worker Identification Card (TWIC).\
<li>Professional Engineer (PE) License Preferred\
</ul>\

<u><strong>Summary:</strong></u><br>\

The Citizen Responder will also monitor compliance with performance standards, provide reports through the CRM system, and will assist with managing the Service Request and Work Order process/application in support of all project divisions.<br>\

<description>

<!\[CDATA\[ <span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;"><strong>Mechanical Engineering Manager</strong></span></span><br>\
<span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;"><strong>Denver, Colorado</strong></span></span><br>\
<span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;"><strong>Direct Hire</strong></span></span><br>\
<span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;"><strong>Salary range: $150-185K</strong></span></span><br>\
<br>\
<span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;"><strong>POSITION SUMMARY:</strong></span></span><br>\
<span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;">The Engineering Manager will lead, develop, and continuously improve the engineering and design team to complete engineering &amp; design efforts towards project design, engineering, procurement, drafting, and product life cycle management of large scale manufactured industrial equipment. </span></span><br>\
<br>\
<span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;"><strong>ESSENTIAL DUTIES AND RESPONSIBILITIES:</strong></span></span>\
<ul>\
<li style="margin-bottom: 0.0in;margin: 0.0in 0.0in 8.0pt;"><span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;">Lead the engineering team on selecting and sizing equipment for fluid handling systems such as pumps, piping, valves, instrumentation, etc.    </span></span>\
<li style="margin: 0.0in 0.0in 8.0pt;"><span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;">Direct team to create 3D SolidWorks layouts (general arrangements), P&amp;IDs, structural drawings, mechanical assembly drawings, and others as needed to support the production floor.   </span></span>\
<li style="margin: 0.0in 0.0in 8.0pt;"><span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;">Coordinate with the manufacturing shop on all fabricated, pre-assembled, and manufactured system designs.</span></span>\
<li style="margin: 0.0in 0.0in 8.0pt;"><span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;">Technical resource and decision-making authority to guide designs for safety, manufacturability, reliability, and within budgets.  </span></span>\
<li style="margin: 0.0in 0.0in 8.0pt;"><span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;">Act as an independent project manager of key accounts as required.</span></span>\
<li style="margin: 0.0in 0.0in 8.0pt;"><span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;">Select engineered equipment to be used in engineered product design.</span></span>\
<li style="margin: 0.0in 0.0in 8.0pt;"><span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;">Review/ create project proposals that accurately depict offerings to our client. </span></span>\
<li style="margin: 0.0in 0.0in 8.0pt;"><span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;">Proficient at guiding facility layouts due to maintenance, reliability, and serviceability needs. </span></span>\
<li style="margin: 0.0in 0.0in 8.0pt;"><span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;">Review mechanical and electrical manufacturing for accuracy and intended function based on the project design. </span></span>\
<li style="margin: 0.0in 0.0in 8.0pt;"><span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;">Liaison between the engineering/ design team and the production team</span></span>\
<li style="margin: 0.0in 0.0in 8.0pt;"><span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;">Coordinate material take-offs for purchase of all materials required for fabrication and installation of provided prefabricated and unitized systems.</span></span>\
<li style="margin: 0.0in 0.0in 8.0pt;"><span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;">Ability to review industry documents to guide designs, including ASME, ANSI, NEC, NFPA, ASTM, customer specifications, and further as required.</span></span>\
</ul>\
<br>\
<span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;"><strong>EDUCATION &amp; EXPERIENCE</strong></span></span>\
\
<ul>\
<li style="margin-bottom: 0.0in;margin: 0.0in 0.0in 8.0pt;"><span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;">Bachelor's degree in mechanical engineering or technical engineering, math, or science is required.</span></span>\
<li style="margin: 0.0in 0.0in 8.0pt;"><span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;">5+ plus years of experience with each of the following:                   </span></span>\
<ul style="list-style-type: circle;">\
<li style="margin: 0.0in 0.0in 8.0pt;"><span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;">Engineering design </span></span>\
<li style="margin: 0.0in 0.0in 8.0pt;"><span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;">Engineering management role with direct reports</span></span>\

<li style="margin: 0.0in 0.0in 8.0pt;"><span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;">Mechanical systems and associated components (i.e. pumps, piping, and instrumentation)</span></span>\
